Pure function stages: extract() — extracts and [GAP] tagged lines into KnowledgeEntry array with MD5 hashes; dedup() — removes entries whose hash already appears in knowledge.md via <!-- hash:hex --> annotations, plus intra-batch dedup; categorize() — keyword classification (fix/resolve/error→fix, pattern/approach/strategy→pattern, [GAP]→gap, rest→context), preserves gap from extraction; persist() — appends to knowledge.md with hash annotations for next-harvest dedup. Exported computeEntryHash, categorizeEntry, extract, dedup, categorize for unit testing. Wrote 19 new TDD tests in test/knowledge.test.ts: computeEntryHash consistency/normalization/hex format, categorizeEntry 4 categories, extract tagged/empty, dedup existing/batch/passthrough, categorize keyword assignment, HarvestPipeline chaining/persist-annotations/dedup-skip/empty/toggle-dedup/skip-persist. tsc --noEmit clean, all 361 tests pass.
- 2026-03-18: [GAP] [2026-03-14T06:06:51.289Z] [29247b90-1338-47f4-9577-c9aff6748f69] Task started: **Compounding knowledge system**: Create `src/knowledge.ts` exporting `KnowledgeManager` class. Constructor accepts `knowledgePath: string` (default `'knowledge.md'`) and `maxInjectLines: number` (default 15). Methods: (1) `extractLearnings(output: string): string[]` — scan text for lines containing `[LEARNING]` tag (case-insensitive), return matched content stripped of the tag prefix; (2) `extractGaps(output: string): string[]` — scan for `` tags, return content; (3) `persist(workspaceRoot, learnings: string[], gaps: string[])` — append timestamped entries to `knowledge.md` under `## Learnings` and `## Gaps` sections, create file with headers if missing; (4) `getRelevantLearnings(workspaceRoot, taskDescription: string): string[]` — read `knowledge.md`, extract all learnings, filter by keyword overlap (split task description into words ≥4 chars, match any learning containing ≥2 of those words), return up to `maxInjectLines` most recent matches. In `src/prompt.ts`, modify `buildPrompt` to accept optional `learnings?: string[]` parameter. When non-empty, insert a `PRIOR LEARNINGS` section after `AVAILABLE CAPABILITIES` containing the filtered learnings as bullet points. In `src/orchestrator.ts`, after each task completion, call `extractLearnings` and `extractGaps` on any captured Copilot output, then `persist`. Before building each task prompt, call `getRelevantLearnings` and pass results to `buildPrompt`. Add `knowledge?: { enabled: boolean; path: string; maxInjectLines: number }` to `RalphConfig` (default `{ enabled: true, path: 'knowledge.md', maxInjectLines: 15 }`). Write tests FIRST in `test/knowledge.test.ts`: extractLearnings finds tagged lines, extractGaps finds tagged lines, persist creates/appends file, getRelevantLearnings filters by keywords, empty input returns empty. Run `npx tsc --noEmit` and `npx vitest run` — ALL tests must pass before marking this checkbox.

Methods: extractLearnings scans for [LEARNING] tags (case-insensitive), extractGaps scans for tags, persist appends timestamped entries to knowledge.md under ## Learnings and ## Gaps sections (creates file with headers if missing), getRelevantLearnings reads knowledge.md, filters learnings by keyword overlap (words >=4 chars, >=2 matches), returns up to maxInjectLines most recent. Modified buildPrompt in prompt.ts to accept optional learnings parameter, renders PRIOR LEARNINGS section after AVAILABLE CAPABILITIES as bullet points. In orchestrator.ts: creates KnowledgeManager in runLoop, gets relevant learnings before building prompt and passes to buildPrompt, extracts learnings/gaps after task completion and persists. - 2026-03-18: [GAP] [2026-03-14] Implemented compounding knowledge system. Created src/knowledge.ts with KnowledgeManager class: constructor accepts knowledgePath (default "knowledge.md") and maxInjectLines (default 15). Methods: extractLearnings scans for [LEARNING] tags (case-insensitive), extractGaps scans for tags, persist appends timestamped entries to knowledge.md under ## Learnings and ## Gaps sections (creates file with headers if missing), getRelevantLearnings reads knowledge.md, filters learnings by keyword overlap (words >=4 chars, >=2 matches), returns up to maxInjectLines most recent. Added KnowledgeConfig interface and DEFAULT_KNOWLEDGE_CONFIG to types.ts, added knowledge? to RalphConfig and DEFAULT_CONFIG. Modified buildPrompt in prompt.ts to accept optional learnings parameter, renders PRIOR LEARNINGS section after AVAILABLE CAPABILITIES as bullet points. In orchestrator.ts: creates KnowledgeManager in runLoop, gets relevant learnings before building prompt and passes to buildPrompt, extracts learnings/gaps after task completion and persists. - 2026-03-18: [GAP] [2026-03-14T06:10:30.861Z] [29247b90-1338-47f4-9577-c9aff6748f69] Task completed: **Compounding knowledge system**: Create `src/knowledge.ts` exporting `KnowledgeManager` class. Constructor accepts `knowledgePath: string` (default `'knowledge.md'`) and `maxInjectLines: number` (default 15). Methods: (1) `extractLearnings(output: string): string[]` — scan text for lines containing `[LEARNING]` tag (case-insensitive), return matched content stripped of the tag prefix; (2) `extractGaps(output: string): string[]` — scan for `` tags, return content; (3) `persist(workspaceRoot, learnings: string[], gaps: string[])` — append timestamped entries to `knowledge.md` under `## Learnings` and `## Gaps` sections, create file with headers if missing; (4) `getRelevantLearnings(workspaceRoot, taskDescription: string): string[]` — read `knowledge.md`, extract all learnings, filter by keyword overlap (split task description into words ≥4 chars, match any learning containing ≥2 of those words), return up to `maxInjectLines` most recent matches. In `src/prompt.ts`, modify `buildPrompt` to accept optional `learnings?: string[]` parameter. When non-empty, insert a `PRIOR LEARNINGS` section after `AVAILABLE CAPABILITIES` containing the filtered learnings as bullet points. In `src/orchestrator.ts`, after each task completion, call `extractLearnings` and `extractGaps` on any captured Copilot output, then `persist`. Before building each task prompt, call `getRelevantLearnings` and pass results to `buildPrompt`. Add `knowledge?: { enabled: boolean; path: string; maxInjectLines: number }` to `RalphConfig` (default `{ enabled: true, path: 'knowledge.md', maxInjectLines: 15 }`). Write tests FIRST in `test/knowledge.test.ts`: extractLearnings finds tagged lines, extractGaps finds tagged lines, persist creates/appends file, getRelevantLearnings filters by keywords, empty input returns empty. Run `npx tsc --noEmit` and `npx vitest run` — ALL tests must pass before marking this checkbox. (220s)
- 2026-03-18: [GAP] [2026-03-16T07:27:00.000Z] [Task-058] Task completed: **Task 58 — Knowledge Harvest Pipeline**: Upgraded KnowledgeManager ingestion to composable pipeline. Added KnowledgeEntry interface to src/types.ts with content, category ('pattern'|'fix'|'context'|'gap'), timestamp, taskId, hash fields. Added HarvestConfig with toggleable stages array (default: ['extract','dedup','categorize','persist'], score opt-in). Added HarvestPipeline class to src/knowledge.ts with run() method chaining stages. Pure function stages: extract() — extracts [LEARNING] and tagged lines into KnowledgeEntry array with MD5 hashes; dedup() — removes entries whose hash already appears in knowledge.md via <!-- hash:hex --> annotations, plus intra-batch dedup; categorize() — keyword classification (fix/resolve/error→fix, pattern/approach/strategy→pattern, [GAP]→gap, rest→context), preserves gap from extraction; persist() — appends to knowledge.md with hash annotations for next-harvest dedup. Exported computeEntryHash, categorizeEntry, extract, dedup, categorize for unit testing. Wrote 19 new TDD tests in test/knowledge.test.ts: computeEntryHash consistency/normalization/hex format, categorizeEntry 4 categories, extract tagged/empty, dedup existing/batch/passthrough, categorize keyword assignment, HarvestPipeline chaining/persist-annotations/dedup-skip/empty/toggle-dedup/skip-persist. tsc --noEmit clean, all 361 tests pass.

Before building each task prompt, call `getRelevantLearnings` and pass results to `buildPrompt`. Add `knowledge?: { enabled: boolean; path: string; maxInjectLines: number }` to `RalphConfig` (default `{ enabled: true, path: 'knowledge.md', maxInjectLines: 15 }`). Write tests FIRST in `test/knowledge.test.ts`: extractLearnings finds tagged lines, extractGaps finds tagged lines, persist creates/appends file, getRelevantLearnings filters by keywords, empty input returns empty. Run `npx tsc --noEmit` and `npx vitest run` — ALL tests must pass before marking this checkbox. (220s)
- 2026-03-18: [GAP] [2026-03-16T07:27:00.000Z] [Task-058] Task completed: **Task 58 — Knowledge Harvest Pipeline**: Upgraded KnowledgeManager ingestion to composable pipeline. Added KnowledgeEntry interface to src/types.ts with content, category ('pattern'|'fix'|'context'|'gap'), timestamp, taskId, hash fields. Added HarvestConfig with toggleable stages array (default: ['extract','dedup','categorize','persist'], score opt-in). Added HarvestPipeline class to src/knowledge.ts with run() method chaining stages. Pure function stages: extract() — extracts [LEARNING] and tagged lines into KnowledgeEntry array with MD5 hashes; dedup() — removes entries whose hash already appears in knowledge.md via <!-- hash:hex --> annotations, plus intra-batch dedup; categorize() — keyword classification (fix/resolve/error→fix, pattern/approach/strategy→pattern, [GAP]→gap, rest→context), preserves gap from extraction; persist() — appends to knowledge.md with hash annotations for next-harvest dedup. Exported computeEntryHash, categorizeEntry, extract, dedup, categorize for unit testing. Wrote 19 new TDD tests in test/knowledge.test.ts: computeEntryHash consistency/normalization/hex format, categorizeEntry 4 categories, extract tagged/empty, dedup existing/batch/passthrough, categorize keyword assignment, HarvestPipeline chaining/persist-annotations/dedup-skip/empty/toggle-dedup/skip-persist. tsc --noEmit clean, all 361 tests pass.
- 2026-03-18: [2026-03-14T06:06:51.289Z] [29247b90-1338-47f4-9577-c9aff6748f69] Task started: **Compounding knowledge system**: Create `src/knowledge.ts` exporting `KnowledgeManager` class. Constructor accepts `knowledgePath: string` (default `'knowledge.md'`) and `maxInjectLines: number` (default 15). Methods: (1) `extractLearnings(output: string): string[]` — scan text for lines containing `` tag (case-insensitive), return matched content stripped of the tag prefix; (2) `extractGaps(output: string): string[]` — scan for `[GAP]` tags, return content; (3) `persist(workspaceRoot, learnings: string[], gaps: string[])` — append timestamped entries to `knowledge.md` under `## Learnings` and `## Gaps` sections, create file with headers if missing; (4) `getRelevantLearnings(workspaceRoot, taskDescription: string): string[]` — read `knowledge.md`, extract all learnings, filter by keyword overlap (split task description into words ≥4 chars, match any learning containing ≥2 of those words), return up to `maxInjectLines` most recent matches. In `src/prompt.ts`, modify `buildPrompt` to accept optional `learnings?: string[]` parameter. Methods: (1) `extractLearnings(output: string): string[]` — scan text for lines containing `` tag (case-insensitive), return matched content stripped of the tag prefix; (2) `extractGaps(output: string): string[]` — scan for `[GAP]` tags, return content; (3) `persist(workspaceRoot, learnings: string[], gaps: string[])` — append timestamped entries to `knowledge.md` under `## Learnings` and `## Gaps` sections, create file with headers if missing; (4) `getRelevantLearnings(workspaceRoot, taskDescription: string): string[]` — read `knowledge.md`, extract all learnings, filter by keyword overlap (split task description into words ≥4 chars, match any learning containing ≥2 of those words), return up to `maxInjectLines` most recent matches. In `src/prompt.ts`, modify `buildPrompt` to accept optional `learnings?: string[]` parameter. When non-empty, insert a `PRIOR LEARNINGS` section after `AVAILABLE CAPABILITIES` containing the filtered learnings as bullet points. In `src/orchestrator.ts`, after each task completion, call `extractLearnings` and `extractGaps` on any captured Copilot output, then `persist`. Before building each task prompt, call `getRelevantLearnings` and pass results to `buildPrompt`. Add `knowledge?: { enabled: boolean; path: string; maxInjectLines: number }` to `RalphConfig` (default `{ enabled: true, path: 'knowledge.md', maxInjectLines: 15 }`). Write tests FIRST in `test/knowledge.test.ts`: extractLearnings finds tagged lines, extractGaps finds tagged lines, persist creates/appends file, getRelevantLearnings filters by keywords, empty input returns empty. Run `npx tsc --noEmit` and `npx vitest run` — ALL tests must pass before marking this checkbox.
- 2026-03-18: [2026-03-14] Implemented compounding knowledge system. Created src/knowledge.ts with KnowledgeManager class: constructor accepts knowledgePath (default "knowledge.md") and maxInjectLines (default 15). Methods: extractLearnings scans for tags (case-insensitive), extractGaps scans for [GAP] tags, persist appends timestamped entries to knowledge.md under ## Learnings and ## Gaps sections (creates file with headers if missing), getRelevantLearnings reads knowledge.md, filters learnings by keyword overlap (words >=4 chars, >=2 matches), returns up to maxInjectLines most recent. Added KnowledgeConfig interface and DEFAULT_KNOWLEDGE_CONFIG to types.ts, added knowledge? to RalphConfig and DEFAULT_CONFIG. Modified buildPrompt in prompt.ts to accept optional learnings parameter, renders PRIOR LEARNINGS section after AVAILABLE CAPABILITIES as bullet points. In orchestrator.ts: creates KnowledgeManager in runLoop, gets relevant learnings before building prompt and passes to buildPrompt, extracts learnings/gaps after task completion and persists. Added knowledge to loadConfig. Wrote 16 TDD tests in test/knowledge.test.ts. tsc --noEmit clean, all 188 tests pass.

- 2026-03-18: [2026-03-16T07:27:00.000Z] [Task-058] Task completed: **Task 58 — Knowledge Harvest Pipeline**: Upgraded KnowledgeManager ingestion to composable pipeline. Added KnowledgeEntry interface to src/types.ts with content, category ('pattern'|'fix'|'context'|'gap'), timestamp, taskId, hash fields. Added HarvestConfig with toggleable stages array (default: ['extract','dedup','categorize','persist'], score opt-in). Added HarvestPipeline class to src/knowledge.ts with run() method chaining stages. Pure function stages: extract() — extracts and [GAP] tagged lines into KnowledgeEntry array with MD5 hashes; dedup() — removes entries whose hash already appears in knowledge.md via <!-- hash:hex --> annotations, plus intra-batch dedup; categorize() — keyword classification (fix/resolve/error→fix, pattern/approach/strategy→pattern, [GAP]→gap, rest→context), preserves gap from extraction; persist() — appends to knowledge.md with hash annotations for next-harvest dedup. Exported computeEntryHash, categorizeEntry, extract, dedup, categorize for unit testing. Wrote 19 new TDD tests in test/knowledge.test.ts: computeEntryHash consistency/normalization/hex format, categorizeEntry 4 categories, extract tagged/empty, dedup existing/batch/passthrough, categorize keyword assignment, HarvestPipeline chaining/persist-annotations/dedup-skip/empty/toggle-dedup/skip-persist. tsc --noEmit clean, all 361 tests pass.

Added knowledge to loadConfig. Wrote 16 TDD tests in test/knowledge.test.ts. tsc --noEmit clean, all 188 tests pass.
- 2026-03-18: [2026-03-14T06:10:30.861Z] [29247b90-1338-47f4-9577-c9aff6748f69] Task completed: **Compounding knowledge system**: Create `src/knowledge.ts` exporting `KnowledgeManager` class. Constructor accepts `knowledgePath: string` (default `'knowledge.md'`) and `maxInjectLines: number` (default 15). Methods: (1) `extractLearnings(output: string): string[]` — scan text for lines containing `` tag (case-insensitive), return matched content stripped of the tag prefix; (2) `extractGaps(output: string): string[]` — scan for `[GAP]` tags, return content; (3) `persist(workspaceRoot, learnings: string[], gaps: string[])` — append timestamped entries to `knowledge.md` under `## Learnings` and `## Gaps` sections, create file with headers if missing; (4) `getRelevantLearnings(workspaceRoot, taskDescription: string): string[]` — read `knowledge.md`, extract all learnings, filter by keyword overlap (split task description into words ≥4 chars, match any learning containing ≥2 of those words), return up to `maxInjectLines` most recent matches. In `src/prompt.ts`, modify `buildPrompt` to accept optional `learnings?: string[]` parameter. When non-empty, insert a `PRIOR LEARNINGS` section after `AVAILABLE CAPABILITIES` containing the filtered learnings as bullet points. In `src/orchestrator.ts`, after each task completion, call `extractLearnings` and `extractGaps` on any captured Copilot output, then `persist`. Before building each task prompt, call `getRelevantLearnings` and pass results to `buildPrompt`. Add `knowledge?: { enabled: boolean; path: string; maxInjectLines: number }` to `RalphConfig` (default `{ enabled: true, path: 'knowledge.md', maxInjectLines: 15 }`). Write tests FIRST in `test/knowledge.test.ts`: extractLearnings finds tagged lines, extractGaps finds tagged lines, persist creates/appends file, getRelevantLearnings filters by keywords, empty input returns empty. Run `npx tsc --noEmit` and `npx vitest run` — ALL tests must pass before marking this checkbox. (220s)
- 2026-03-18: [2026-03-16T07:27:00.000Z] [Task-058] Task completed: **Task 58 — Knowledge Harvest Pipeline**: Upgraded KnowledgeManager ingestion to composable pipeline. Added KnowledgeEntry interface to src/types.ts with content, category ('pattern'|'fix'|'context'|'gap'), timestamp, taskId, hash fields. Added HarvestConfig with toggleable stages array (default: ['extract','dedup','categorize','persist'], score opt-in). Added HarvestPipeline class to src/knowledge.ts with run() method chaining stages. Pure function stages: extract() — extracts and [GAP] tagged lines into KnowledgeEntry array with MD5 hashes; dedup() — removes entries whose hash already appears in knowledge.md via <!-- hash:hex --> annotations, plus intra-batch dedup; categorize() — keyword classification (fix/resolve/error→fix, pattern/approach/strategy→pattern, [GAP]→gap, rest→context), preserves gap from extraction; persist() — appends to knowledge.md with hash annotations for next-harvest dedup. Exported computeEntryHash, categorizeEntry, extract, dedup, categorize for unit testing. Wrote 19 new TDD tests in test/knowledge.test.ts: computeEntryHash consistency/normalization/hex format, categorizeEntry 4 categories, extract tagged/empty, dedup existing/batch/passthrough, categorize keyword assignment, HarvestPipeline chaining/persist-annotations/dedup-skip/empty/toggle-dedup/skip-persist. tsc --noEmit clean, all 361 tests pass.

Pure function stages: extract() — extracts and [GAP] tagged lines into KnowledgeEntry array with MD5 hashes; dedup() — removes entries whose hash already appears in knowledge.md via <!-- hash:hex --> annotations, plus intra-batch dedup; categorize() — keyword classification (fix/resolve/error→fix, pattern/approach/strategy→pattern, [GAP]→gap, rest→context), preserves gap from extraction; persist() — appends to knowledge.md with hash annotations for next-harvest dedup. Exported computeEntryHash, categorizeEntry, extract, dedup, categorize for unit testing. Wrote 19 new TDD tests in test/knowledge.test.ts: computeEntryHash consistency/normalization/hex format, categorizeEntry 4 categories, extract tagged/empty, dedup existing/batch/passthrough, categorize keyword assignment, HarvestPipeline chaining/persist-annotations/dedup-skip/empty/toggle-dedup/skip-persist. tsc --noEmit clean, all 361 tests pass.
- 2026-03-20: [GAP] [2026-03-14T06:06:51.289Z] [29247b90-1338-47f4-9577-c9aff6748f69] Task started: **Compounding knowledge system**: Create `src/knowledge.ts` exporting `KnowledgeManager` class. Constructor accepts `knowledgePath: string` (default `'knowledge.md'`) and `maxInjectLines: number` (default 15). Methods: (1) `extractLearnings(output: string): string[]` — scan text for lines containing `[LEARNING]` tag (case-insensitive), return matched content stripped of the tag prefix; (2) `extractGaps(output: string): string[]` — scan for `` tags, return content; (3) `persist(workspaceRoot, learnings: string[], gaps: string[])` — append timestamped entries to `knowledge.md` under `## Learnings` and `## Gaps` sections, create file with headers if missing; (4) `getRelevantLearnings(workspaceRoot, taskDescription: string): string[]` — read `knowledge.md`, extract all learnings, filter by keyword overlap (split task description into words ≥4 chars, match any learning containing ≥2 of those words), return up to `maxInjectLines` most recent matches. In `src/prompt.ts`, modify `buildPrompt` to accept optional `learnings?: string[]` parameter. When non-empty, insert a `PRIOR LEARNINGS` section after `AVAILABLE CAPABILITIES` containing the filtered learnings as bullet points. In `src/orchestrator.ts`, after each task completion, call `extractLearnings` and `extractGaps` on any captured Copilot output, then `persist`. Before building each task prompt, call `getRelevantLearnings` and pass results to `buildPrompt`. Add `knowledge?: { enabled: boolean; path: string; maxInjectLines: number }` to `RalphConfig` (default `{ enabled: true, path: 'knowledge.md', maxInjectLines: 15 }`). Write tests FIRST in `test/knowledge.test.ts`: extractLearnings finds tagged lines, extractGaps finds tagged lines, persist creates/appends file, getRelevantLearnings filters by keywords, empty input returns empty. Run `npx tsc --noEmit` and `npx vitest run` — ALL tests must pass before marking this checkbox.

Methods: extractLearnings scans for [LEARNING] tags (case-insensitive), extractGaps scans for tags, persist appends timestamped entries to knowledge.md under ## Learnings and ## Gaps sections (creates file with headers if missing), getRelevantLearnings reads knowledge.md, filters learnings by keyword overlap (words >=4 chars, >=2 matches), returns up to maxInjectLines most recent. Modified buildPrompt in prompt.ts to accept optional learnings parameter, renders PRIOR LEARNINGS section after AVAILABLE CAPABILITIES as bullet points. In orchestrator.ts: creates KnowledgeManager in runLoop, gets relevant learnings before building prompt and passes to buildPrompt, extracts learnings/gaps after task completion and persists. - 2026-03-20: [GAP] [2026-03-14] Implemented compounding knowledge system. Created src/knowledge.ts with KnowledgeManager class: constructor accepts knowledgePath (default "knowledge.md") and maxInjectLines (default 15). Methods: extractLearnings scans for [LEARNING] tags (case-insensitive), extractGaps scans for tags, persist appends timestamped entries to knowledge.md under ## Learnings and ## Gaps sections (creates file with headers if missing), getRelevantLearnings reads knowledge.md, filters learnings by keyword overlap (words >=4 chars, >=2 matches), returns up to maxInjectLines most recent. Added KnowledgeConfig interface and DEFAULT_KNOWLEDGE_CONFIG to types.ts, added knowledge? to RalphConfig and DEFAULT_CONFIG. Modified buildPrompt in prompt.ts to accept optional learnings parameter, renders PRIOR LEARNINGS section after AVAILABLE CAPABILITIES as bullet points. In orchestrator.ts: creates KnowledgeManager in runLoop, gets relevant learnings before building prompt and passes to buildPrompt, extracts learnings/gaps after task completion and persists. - 2026-03-20: [GAP] [2026-03-14T06:10:30.861Z] [29247b90-1338-47f4-9577-c9aff6748f69] Task completed: **Compounding knowledge system**: Create `src/knowledge.ts` exporting `KnowledgeManager` class. Constructor accepts `knowledgePath: string` (default `'knowledge.md'`) and `maxInjectLines: number` (default 15). Methods: (1) `extractLearnings(output: string): string[]` — scan text for lines containing `[LEARNING]` tag (case-insensitive), return matched content stripped of the tag prefix; (2) `extractGaps(output: string): string[]` — scan for `` tags, return content; (3) `persist(workspaceRoot, learnings: string[], gaps: string[])` — append timestamped entries to `knowledge.md` under `## Learnings` and `## Gaps` sections, create file with headers if missing; (4) `getRelevantLearnings(workspaceRoot, taskDescription: string): string[]` — read `knowledge.md`, extract all learnings, filter by keyword overlap (split task description into words ≥4 chars, match any learning containing ≥2 of those words), return up to `maxInjectLines` most recent matches. In `src/prompt.ts`, modify `buildPrompt` to accept optional `learnings?: string[]` parameter. When non-empty, insert a `PRIOR LEARNINGS` section after `AVAILABLE CAPABILITIES` containing the filtered learnings as bullet points. In `src/orchestrator.ts`, after each task completion, call `extractLearnings` and `extractGaps` on any captured Copilot output, then `persist`. Before building each task prompt, call `getRelevantLearnings` and pass results to `buildPrompt`. Add `knowledge?: { enabled: boolean; path: string; maxInjectLines: number }` to `RalphConfig` (default `{ enabled: true, path: 'knowledge.md', maxInjectLines: 15 }`). Write tests FIRST in `test/knowledge.test.ts`: extractLearnings finds tagged lines, extractGaps finds tagged lines, persist creates/appends file, getRelevantLearnings filters by keywords, empty input returns empty. Run `npx tsc --noEmit` and `npx vitest run` — ALL tests must pass before marking this checkbox. (220s)
- 2026-03-20: [GAP] [2026-03-16T07:27:00.000Z] [Task-058] Task completed: **Task 58 — Knowledge Harvest Pipeline**: Upgraded KnowledgeManager ingestion to composable pipeline. Added KnowledgeEntry interface to src/types.ts with content, category ('pattern'|'fix'|'context'|'gap'), timestamp, taskId, hash fields. Added HarvestConfig with toggleable stages array (default: ['extract','dedup','categorize','persist'], score opt-in). Added HarvestPipeline class to src/knowledge.ts with run() method chaining stages. Pure function stages: extract() — extracts [LEARNING] and tagged lines into KnowledgeEntry array with MD5 hashes; dedup() — removes entries whose hash already appears in knowledge.md via <!-- hash:hex --> annotations, plus intra-batch dedup; categorize() — keyword classification (fix/resolve/error→fix, pattern/approach/strategy→pattern, [GAP]→gap, rest→context), preserves gap from extraction; persist() — appends to knowledge.md with hash annotations for next-harvest dedup. Exported computeEntryHash, categorizeEntry, extract, dedup, categorize for unit testing. Wrote 19 new TDD tests in test/knowledge.test.ts: computeEntryHash consistency/normalization/hex format, categorizeEntry 4 categories, extract tagged/empty, dedup existing/batch/passthrough, categorize keyword assignment, HarvestPipeline chaining/persist-annotations/dedup-skip/empty/toggle-dedup/skip-persist. tsc --noEmit clean, all 361 tests pass.

Before building each task prompt, call `getRelevantLearnings` and pass results to `buildPrompt`. Add `knowledge?: { enabled: boolean; path: string; maxInjectLines: number }` to `RalphConfig` (default `{ enabled: true, path: 'knowledge.md', maxInjectLines: 15 }`). Write tests FIRST in `test/knowledge.test.ts`: extractLearnings finds tagged lines, extractGaps finds tagged lines, persist creates/appends file, getRelevantLearnings filters by keywords, empty input returns empty. Run `npx tsc --noEmit` and `npx vitest run` — ALL tests must pass before marking this checkbox. (220s)
- 2026-03-20: [GAP] [2026-03-16T07:27:00.000Z] [Task-058] Task completed: **Task 58 — Knowledge Harvest Pipeline**: Upgraded KnowledgeManager ingestion to composable pipeline. Added KnowledgeEntry interface to src/types.ts with content, category ('pattern'|'fix'|'context'|'gap'), timestamp, taskId, hash fields. Added HarvestConfig with toggleable stages array (default: ['extract','dedup','categorize','persist'], score opt-in). Added HarvestPipeline class to src/knowledge.ts with run() method chaining stages. Pure function stages: extract() — extracts [LEARNING] and tagged lines into KnowledgeEntry array with MD5 hashes; dedup() — removes entries whose hash already appears in knowledge.md via <!-- hash:hex --> annotations, plus intra-batch dedup; categorize() — keyword classification (fix/resolve/error→fix, pattern/approach/strategy→pattern, [GAP]→gap, rest→context), preserves gap from extraction; persist() — appends to knowledge.md with hash annotations for next-harvest dedup. Exported computeEntryHash, categorizeEntry, extract, dedup, categorize for unit testing. Wrote 19 new TDD tests in test/knowledge.test.ts: computeEntryHash consistency/normalization/hex format, categorizeEntry 4 categories, extract tagged/empty, dedup existing/batch/passthrough, categorize keyword assignment, HarvestPipeline chaining/persist-annotations/dedup-skip/empty/toggle-dedup/skip-persist. tsc --noEmit clean, all 361 tests pass.
- 2026-03-20: [2026-03-14T06:06:51.289Z] [29247b90-1338-47f4-9577-c9aff6748f69] Task started: **Compounding knowledge system**: Create `src/knowledge.ts` exporting `KnowledgeManager` class. Constructor accepts `knowledgePath: string` (default `'knowledge.md'`) and `maxInjectLines: number` (default 15). Methods: (1) `extractLearnings(output: string): string[]` — scan text for lines containing `` tag (case-insensitive), return matched content stripped of the tag prefix; (2) `extractGaps(output: string): string[]` — scan for `[GAP]` tags, return content; (3) `persist(workspaceRoot, learnings: string[], gaps: string[])` — append timestamped entries to `knowledge.md` under `## Learnings` and `## Gaps` sections, create file with headers if missing; (4) `getRelevantLearnings(workspaceRoot, taskDescription: string): string[]` — read `knowledge.md`, extract all learnings, filter by keyword overlap (split task description into words ≥4 chars, match any learning containing ≥2 of those words), return up to `maxInjectLines` most recent matches. In `src/prompt.ts`, modify `buildPrompt` to accept optional `learnings?: string[]` parameter. Before building each task prompt, call `getRelevantLearnings` and pass results to `buildPrompt`. Methods: (1) `extractLearnings(output: string): string[]` — scan text for lines containing `` tag (case-insensitive), return matched content stripped of the tag prefix; (2) `extractGaps(output: string): string[]` — scan for `[GAP]` tags, return content; (3) `persist(workspaceRoot, learnings: string[], gaps: string[])` — append timestamped entries to `knowledge.md` under `## Learnings` and `## Gaps` sections, create file with headers if missing; (4) `getRelevantLearnings(workspaceRoot, taskDescription: string): string[]` — read `knowledge.md`, extract all learnings, filter by keyword overlap (split task description into words ≥4 chars, match any learning containing ≥2 of those words), return up to `maxInjectLines` most recent matches. In `src/prompt.ts`, modify `buildPrompt` to accept optional `learnings?: string[]` parameter. When non-empty, insert a `PRIOR LEARNINGS` section after `AVAILABLE CAPABILITIES` containing the filtered learnings as bullet points. In `src/orchestrator.ts`, after each task completion, call `extractLearnings` and `extractGaps` on any captured Copilot output, then `persist`. Before building each task prompt, call `getRelevantLearnings` and pass results to `buildPrompt`. Add `knowledge?: { enabled: boolean; path: string; maxInjectLines: number }` to `RalphConfig` (default `{ enabled: true, path: 'knowledge.md', maxInjectLines: 15 }`). Write tests FIRST in `test/knowledge.test.ts`: extractLearnings finds tagged lines, extractGaps finds tagged lines, persist creates/appends file, getRelevantLearnings filters by keywords, empty input returns empty. Run `npx tsc --noEmit` and `npx vitest run` — ALL tests must pass before marking this checkbox.
- 2026-03-20: [2026-03-14] Implemented compounding knowledge system. Created src/knowledge.ts with KnowledgeManager class: constructor accepts knowledgePath (default "knowledge.md") and maxInjectLines (default 15). Methods: extractLearnings scans for tags (case-insensitive), extractGaps scans for [GAP] tags, persist appends timestamped entries to knowledge.md under ## Learnings and ## Gaps sections (creates file with headers if missing), getRelevantLearnings reads knowledge.md, filters learnings by keyword overlap (words >=4 chars, >=2 matches), returns up to maxInjectLines most recent. Added KnowledgeConfig interface and DEFAULT_KNOWLEDGE_CONFIG to types.ts, added knowledge? to RalphConfig and DEFAULT_CONFIG. Modified buildPrompt in prompt.ts to accept optional learnings parameter, renders PRIOR LEARNINGS section after AVAILABLE CAPABILITIES as bullet points. In orchestrator.ts: creates KnowledgeManager in runLoop, gets relevant learnings before building prompt and passes to buildPrompt, extracts learnings/gaps after task completion and persists. Added knowledge to loadConfig. Wrote 16 TDD tests in test/knowledge.test.ts. tsc --noEmit clean, all 188 tests pass.

- 2026-03-20: [2026-03-16T07:27:00.000Z] [Task-058] Task completed: **Task 58 — Knowledge Harvest Pipeline**: Upgraded KnowledgeManager ingestion to composable pipeline. Added KnowledgeEntry interface to src/types.ts with content, category ('pattern'|'fix'|'context'|'gap'), timestamp, taskId, hash fields. Added HarvestConfig with toggleable stages array (default: ['extract','dedup','categorize','persist'], score opt-in). Added HarvestPipeline class to src/knowledge.ts with run() method chaining stages. Pure function stages: extract() — extracts and [GAP] tagged lines into KnowledgeEntry array with MD5 hashes; dedup() — removes entries whose hash already appears in knowledge.md via <!-- hash:hex --> annotations, plus intra-batch dedup; categorize() — keyword classification (fix/resolve/error→fix, pattern/approach/strategy→pattern, [GAP]→gap, rest→context), preserves gap from extraction; persist() — appends to knowledge.md with hash annotations for next-harvest dedup. Exported computeEntryHash, categorizeEntry, extract, dedup, categorize for unit testing. Wrote 19 new TDD tests in test/knowledge.test.ts: computeEntryHash consistency/normalization/hex format, categorizeEntry 4 categories, extract tagged/empty, dedup existing/batch/passthrough, categorize keyword assignment, HarvestPipeline chaining/persist-annotations/dedup-skip/empty/toggle-dedup/skip-persist. tsc --noEmit clean, all 361 tests pass.

Added knowledge to loadConfig. Wrote 16 TDD tests in test/knowledge.test.ts. tsc --noEmit clean, all 188 tests pass.
- 2026-03-21: [2026-03-14T06:10:30.861Z] [29247b90-1338-47f4-9577-c9aff6748f69] Task completed: **Compounding knowledge system**: Create `src/knowledge.ts` exporting `KnowledgeManager` class. Constructor accepts `knowledgePath: string` (default `'knowledge.md'`) and `maxInjectLines: number` (default 15). Methods: (1) `extractLearnings(output: string): string[]` — scan text for lines containing `` tag (case-insensitive), return matched content stripped of the tag prefix; (2) `extractGaps(output: string): string[]` — scan for `[GAP]` tags, return content; (3) `persist(workspaceRoot, learnings: string[], gaps: string[])` — append timestamped entries to `knowledge.md` under `## Learnings` and `## Gaps` sections, create file with headers if missing; (4) `getRelevantLearnings(workspaceRoot, taskDescription: string): string[]` — read `knowledge.md`, extract all learnings, filter by keyword overlap (split task description into words ≥4 chars, match any learning containing ≥2 of those words), return up to `maxInjectLines` most recent matches. In `src/prompt.ts`, modify `buildPrompt` to accept optional `learnings?: string[]` parameter. When non-empty, insert a `PRIOR LEARNINGS` section after `AVAILABLE CAPABILITIES` containing the filtered learnings as bullet points. In `src/orchestrator.ts`, after each task completion, call `extractLearnings` and `extractGaps` on any captured Copilot output, then `persist`. Before building each task prompt, call `getRelevantLearnings` and pass results to `buildPrompt`. Add `knowledge?: { enabled: boolean; path: string; maxInjectLines: number }` to `RalphConfig` (default `{ enabled: true, path: 'knowledge.md', maxInjectLines: 15 }`). Write tests FIRST in `test/knowledge.test.ts`: extractLearnings finds tagged lines, extractGaps finds tagged lines, persist creates/appends file, getRelevantLearnings filters by keywords, empty input returns empty. Run `npx tsc --noEmit` and `npx vitest run` — ALL tests must pass before marking this checkbox. (220s)
- 2026-03-21: [2026-03-16T07:27:00.000Z] [Task-058] Task completed: **Task 58 — Knowledge Harvest Pipeline**: Upgraded KnowledgeManager ingestion to composable pipeline. Added KnowledgeEntry interface to src/types.ts with content, category ('pattern'|'fix'|'context'|'gap'), timestamp, taskId, hash fields. Added HarvestConfig with toggleable stages array (default: ['extract','dedup','categorize','persist'], score opt-in). Added HarvestPipeline class to src/knowledge.ts with run() method chaining stages. Pure function stages: extract() — extracts and [GAP] tagged lines into KnowledgeEntry array with MD5 hashes; dedup() — removes entries whose hash already appears in knowledge.md via <!-- hash:hex --> annotations, plus intra-batch dedup; categorize() — keyword classification (fix/resolve/error→fix, pattern/approach/strategy→pattern, [GAP]→gap, rest→context), preserves gap from extraction; persist() — appends to knowledge.md with hash annotations for next-harvest dedup. Exported computeEntryHash, categorizeEntry, extract, dedup, categorize for unit testing. Wrote 19 new TDD tests in test/knowledge.test.ts: computeEntryHash consistency/normalization/hex format, categorizeEntry 4 categories, extract tagged/empty, dedup existing/batch/passthrough, categorize keyword assignment, HarvestPipeline chaining/persist-annotations/dedup-skip/empty/toggle-dedup/skip-persist. tsc --noEmit clean, all 361 tests pass.

Pure function stages: extract() — extracts and [GAP] tagged lines into KnowledgeEntry array with MD5 hashes; dedup() — removes entries whose hash already appears in knowledge.md via <!-- hash:hex --> annotations, plus intra-batch dedup; categorize() — keyword classification (fix/resolve/error→fix, pattern/approach/strategy→pattern, [GAP]→gap, rest→context), preserves gap from extraction; persist() — appends to knowledge.md with hash annotations for next-harvest dedup. Exported computeEntryHash, categorizeEntry, extract, dedup, categorize for unit testing. Wrote 19 new TDD tests in test/knowledge.test.ts: computeEntryHash consistency/normalization/hex format, categorizeEntry 4 categories, extract tagged/empty, dedup existing/batch/passthrough, categorize keyword assignment, HarvestPipeline chaining/persist-annotations/dedup-skip/empty/toggle-dedup/skip-persist. tsc --noEmit clean, all 361 tests pass.
- 2026-03-21: [GAP] [2026-03-14T06:06:51.289Z] [29247b90-1338-47f4-9577-c9aff6748f69] Task started: **Compounding knowledge system**: Create `src/knowledge.ts` exporting `KnowledgeManager` class. Constructor accepts `knowledgePath: string` (default `'knowledge.md'`) and `maxInjectLines: number` (default 15). Methods: (1) `extractLearnings(output: string): string[]` — scan text for lines containing `[LEARNING]` tag (case-insensitive), return matched content stripped of the tag prefix; (2) `extractGaps(output: string): string[]` — scan for `` tags, return content; (3) `persist(workspaceRoot, learnings: string[], gaps: string[])` — append timestamped entries to `knowledge.md` under `## Learnings` and `## Gaps` sections, create file with headers if missing; (4) `getRelevantLearnings(workspaceRoot, taskDescription: string): string[]` — read `knowledge.md`, extract all learnings, filter by keyword overlap (split task description into words ≥4 chars, match any learning containing ≥2 of those words), return up to `maxInjectLines` most recent matches. In `src/prompt.ts`, modify `buildPrompt` to accept optional `learnings?: string[]` parameter. When non-empty, insert a `PRIOR LEARNINGS` section after `AVAILABLE CAPABILITIES` containing the filtered learnings as bullet points. In `src/orchestrator.ts`, after each task completion, call `extractLearnings` and `extractGaps` on any captured Copilot output, then `persist`. Before building each task prompt, call `getRelevantLearnings` and pass results to `buildPrompt`. Add `knowledge?: { enabled: boolean; path: string; maxInjectLines: number }` to `RalphConfig` (default `{ enabled: true, path: 'knowledge.md', maxInjectLines: 15 }`). Write tests FIRST in `test/knowledge.test.ts`: extractLearnings finds tagged lines, extractGaps finds tagged lines, persist creates/appends file, getRelevantLearnings filters by keywords, empty input returns empty. Run `npx tsc --noEmit` and `npx vitest run` — ALL tests must pass before marking this checkbox.

Methods: extractLearnings scans for [LEARNING] tags (case-insensitive), extractGaps scans for tags, persist appends timestamped entries to knowledge.md under ## Learnings and ## Gaps sections (creates file with headers if missing), getRelevantLearnings reads knowledge.md, filters learnings by keyword overlap (words >=4 chars, >=2 matches), returns up to maxInjectLines most recent. Modified buildPrompt in prompt.ts to accept optional learnings parameter, renders PRIOR LEARNINGS section after AVAILABLE CAPABILITIES as bullet points. In orchestrator.ts: creates KnowledgeManager in runLoop, gets relevant learnings before building prompt and passes to buildPrompt, extracts learnings/gaps after task completion and persists. - 2026-03-21: [GAP] [2026-03-14] Implemented compounding knowledge system. Created src/knowledge.ts with KnowledgeManager class: constructor accepts knowledgePath (default "knowledge.md") and maxInjectLines (default 15). Methods: extractLearnings scans for [LEARNING] tags (case-insensitive), extractGaps scans for tags, persist appends timestamped entries to knowledge.md under ## Learnings and ## Gaps sections (creates file with headers if missing), getRelevantLearnings reads knowledge.md, filters learnings by keyword overlap (words >=4 chars, >=2 matches), returns up to maxInjectLines most recent. Added KnowledgeConfig interface and DEFAULT_KNOWLEDGE_CONFIG to types.ts, added knowledge? to RalphConfig and DEFAULT_CONFIG. Modified buildPrompt in prompt.ts to accept optional learnings parameter, renders PRIOR LEARNINGS section after AVAILABLE CAPABILITIES as bullet points. In orchestrator.ts: creates KnowledgeManager in runLoop, gets relevant learnings before building prompt and passes to buildPrompt, extracts learnings/gaps after task completion and persists. - 2026-03-21: [GAP] [2026-03-14T06:10:30.861Z] [29247b90-1338-47f4-9577-c9aff6748f69] Task completed: **Compounding knowledge system**: Create `src/knowledge.ts` exporting `KnowledgeManager` class. Constructor accepts `knowledgePath: string` (default `'knowledge.md'`) and `maxInjectLines: number` (default 15). Methods: (1) `extractLearnings(output: string): string[]` — scan text for lines containing `[LEARNING]` tag (case-insensitive), return matched content stripped of the tag prefix; (2) `extractGaps(output: string): string[]` — scan for `` tags, return content; (3) `persist(workspaceRoot, learnings: string[], gaps: string[])` — append timestamped entries to `knowledge.md` under `## Learnings` and `## Gaps` sections, create file with headers if missing; (4) `getRelevantLearnings(workspaceRoot, taskDescription: string): string[]` — read `knowledge.md`, extract all learnings, filter by keyword overlap (split task description into words ≥4 chars, match any learning containing ≥2 of those words), return up to `maxInjectLines` most recent matches. In `src/prompt.ts`, modify `buildPrompt` to accept optional `learnings?: string[]` parameter. When non-empty, insert a `PRIOR LEARNINGS` section after `AVAILABLE CAPABILITIES` containing the filtered learnings as bullet points. In `src/orchestrator.ts`, after each task completion, call `extractLearnings` and `extractGaps` on any captured Copilot output, then `persist`. Before building each task prompt, call `getRelevantLearnings` and pass results to `buildPrompt`. Add `knowledge?: { enabled: boolean; path: string; maxInjectLines: number }` to `RalphConfig` (default `{ enabled: true, path: 'knowledge.md', maxInjectLines: 15 }`). Write tests FIRST in `test/knowledge.test.ts`: extractLearnings finds tagged lines, extractGaps finds tagged lines, persist creates/appends file, getRelevantLearnings filters by keywords, empty input returns empty. Run `npx tsc --noEmit` and `npx vitest run` — ALL tests must pass before marking this checkbox. (220s)
- 2026-03-21: [GAP] [2026-03-16T07:27:00.000Z] [Task-058] Task completed: **Task 58 — Knowledge Harvest Pipeline**: Upgraded KnowledgeManager ingestion to composable pipeline. Added KnowledgeEntry interface to src/types.ts with content, category ('pattern'|'fix'|'context'|'gap'), timestamp, taskId, hash fields. Added HarvestConfig with toggleable stages array (default: ['extract','dedup','categorize','persist'], score opt-in). Added HarvestPipeline class to src/knowledge.ts with run() method chaining stages. Pure function stages: extract() — extracts [LEARNING] and tagged lines into KnowledgeEntry array with MD5 hashes; dedup() — removes entries whose hash already appears in knowledge.md via <!-- hash:hex --> annotations, plus intra-batch dedup; categorize() — keyword classification (fix/resolve/error→fix, pattern/approach/strategy→pattern, [GAP]→gap, rest→context), preserves gap from extraction; persist() — appends to knowledge.md with hash annotations for next-harvest dedup. Exported computeEntryHash, categorizeEntry, extract, dedup, categorize for unit testing. Wrote 19 new TDD tests in test/knowledge.test.ts: computeEntryHash consistency/normalization/hex format, categorizeEntry 4 categories, extract tagged/empty, dedup existing/batch/passthrough, categorize keyword assignment, HarvestPipeline chaining/persist-annotations/dedup-skip/empty/toggle-dedup/skip-persist. tsc --noEmit clean, all 361 tests pass.

Before building each task prompt, call `getRelevantLearnings` and pass results to `buildPrompt`. Add `knowledge?: { enabled: boolean; path: string; maxInjectLines: number }` to `RalphConfig` (default `{ enabled: true, path: 'knowledge.md', maxInjectLines: 15 }`). Write tests FIRST in `test/knowledge.test.ts`: extractLearnings finds tagged lines, extractGaps finds tagged lines, persist creates/appends file, getRelevantLearnings filters by keywords, empty input returns empty. Run `npx tsc --noEmit` and `npx vitest run` — ALL tests must pass before marking this checkbox. (220s)
- 2026-03-21: [GAP] [2026-03-16T07:27:00.000Z] [Task-058] Task completed: **Task 58 — Knowledge Harvest Pipeline**: Upgraded KnowledgeManager ingestion to composable pipeline. Added KnowledgeEntry interface to src/types.ts with content, category ('pattern'|'fix'|'context'|'gap'), timestamp, taskId, hash fields. Added HarvestConfig with toggleable stages array (default: ['extract','dedup','categorize','persist'], score opt-in). Added HarvestPipeline class to src/knowledge.ts with run() method chaining stages. Pure function stages: extract() — extracts [LEARNING] and tagged lines into KnowledgeEntry array with MD5 hashes; dedup() — removes entries whose hash already appears in knowledge.md via <!-- hash:hex --> annotations, plus intra-batch dedup; categorize() — keyword classification (fix/resolve/error→fix, pattern/approach/strategy→pattern, [GAP]→gap, rest→context), preserves gap from extraction; persist() — appends to knowledge.md with hash annotations for next-harvest dedup. Exported computeEntryHash, categorizeEntry, extract, dedup, categorize for unit testing. Wrote 19 new TDD tests in test/knowledge.test.ts: computeEntryHash consistency/normalization/hex format, categorizeEntry 4 categories, extract tagged/empty, dedup existing/batch/passthrough, categorize keyword assignment, HarvestPipeline chaining/persist-annotations/dedup-skip/empty/toggle-dedup/skip-persist. tsc --noEmit clean, all 361 tests pass.
- 2026-03-21: [2026-03-14T06:06:51.289Z] [29247b90-1338-47f4-9577-c9aff6748f69] Task started: **Compounding knowledge system**: Create `src/knowledge.ts` exporting `KnowledgeManager` class. Constructor accepts `knowledgePath: string` (default `'knowledge.md'`) and `maxInjectLines: number` (default 15). Methods: (1) `extractLearnings(output: string): string[]` — scan text for lines containing `` tag (case-insensitive), return matched content stripped of the tag prefix; (2) `extractGaps(output: string): string[]` — scan for `[GAP]` tags, return content; (3) `persist(workspaceRoot, learnings: string[], gaps: string[])` — append timestamped entries to `knowledge.md` under `## Learnings` and `## Gaps` sections, create file with headers if missing; (4) `getRelevantLearnings(workspaceRoot, taskDescription: string): string[]` — read `knowledge.md`, extract all learnings, filter by keyword overlap (split task description into words ≥4 chars, match any learning containing ≥2 of those words), return up to `maxInjectLines` most recent matches. In `src/prompt.ts`, modify `buildPrompt` to accept optional `learnings?: string[]` parameter. Methods: (1) `extractLearnings(output: string): string[]` — scan text for lines containing `` tag (case-insensitive), return matched content stripped of the tag prefix; (2) `extractGaps(output: string): string[]` — scan for `[GAP]` tags, return content; (3) `persist(workspaceRoot, learnings: string[], gaps: string[])` — append timestamped entries to `knowledge.md` under `## Learnings` and `## Gaps` sections, create file with headers if missing; (4) `getRelevantLearnings(workspaceRoot, taskDescription: string): string[]` — read `knowledge.md`, extract all learnings, filter by keyword overlap (split task description into words ≥4 chars, match any learning containing ≥2 of those words), return up to `maxInjectLines` most recent matches. In `src/prompt.ts`, modify `buildPrompt` to accept optional `learnings?: string[]` parameter. When non-empty, insert a `PRIOR LEARNINGS` section after `AVAILABLE CAPABILITIES` containing the filtered learnings as bullet points. In `src/orchestrator.ts`, after each task completion, call `extractLearnings` and `extractGaps` on any captured Copilot output, then `persist`. Before building each task prompt, call `getRelevantLearnings` and pass results to `buildPrompt`. Add `knowledge?: { enabled: boolean; path: string; maxInjectLines: number }` to `RalphConfig` (default `{ enabled: true, path: 'knowledge.md', maxInjectLines: 15 }`). Write tests FIRST in `test/knowledge.test.ts`: extractLearnings finds tagged lines, extractGaps finds tagged lines, persist creates/appends file, getRelevantLearnings filters by keywords, empty input returns empty. Run `npx tsc --noEmit` and `npx vitest run` — ALL tests must pass before marking this checkbox.
- 2026-03-21: [2026-03-14] Implemented compounding knowledge system. Created src/knowledge.ts with KnowledgeManager class: constructor accepts knowledgePath (default "knowledge.md") and maxInjectLines (default 15). Methods: extractLearnings scans for tags (case-insensitive), extractGaps scans for [GAP] tags, persist appends timestamped entries to knowledge.md under ## Learnings and ## Gaps sections (creates file with headers if missing), getRelevantLearnings reads knowledge.md, filters learnings by keyword overlap (words >=4 chars, >=2 matches), returns up to maxInjectLines most recent. Added KnowledgeConfig interface and DEFAULT_KNOWLEDGE_CONFIG to types.ts, added knowledge? to RalphConfig and DEFAULT_CONFIG. Modified buildPrompt in prompt.ts to accept optional learnings parameter, renders PRIOR LEARNINGS section after AVAILABLE CAPABILITIES as bullet points. In orchestrator.ts: creates KnowledgeManager in runLoop, gets relevant learnings before building prompt and passes to buildPrompt, extracts learnings/gaps after task completion and persists. Added knowledge to loadConfig. Wrote 16 TDD tests in test/knowledge.test.ts. tsc --noEmit clean, all 188 tests pass.

- 2026-03-21: [2026-03-16T07:27:00.000Z] [Task-058] Task completed: **Task 58 — Knowledge Harvest Pipeline**: Upgraded KnowledgeManager ingestion to composable pipeline. Added KnowledgeEntry interface to src/types.ts with content, category ('pattern'|'fix'|'context'|'gap'), timestamp, taskId, hash fields. Added HarvestConfig with toggleable stages array (default: ['extract','dedup','categorize','persist'], score opt-in). Added HarvestPipeline class to src/knowledge.ts with run() method chaining stages. Pure function stages: extract() — extracts and [GAP] tagged lines into KnowledgeEntry array with MD5 hashes; dedup() — removes entries whose hash already appears in knowledge.md via <!-- hash:hex --> annotations, plus intra-batch dedup; categorize() — keyword classification (fix/resolve/error→fix, pattern/approach/strategy→pattern, [GAP]→gap, rest→context), preserves gap from extraction; persist() — appends to knowledge.md with hash annotations for next-harvest dedup. Exported computeEntryHash, categorizeEntry, extract, dedup, categorize for unit testing. Wrote 19 new TDD tests in test/knowledge.test.ts: computeEntryHash consistency/normalization/hex format, categorizeEntry 4 categories, extract tagged/empty, dedup existing/batch/passthrough, categorize keyword assignment, HarvestPipeline chaining/persist-annotations/dedup-skip/empty/toggle-dedup/skip-persist. tsc --noEmit clean, all 361 tests pass.
